        LEFT OUTER JOIN [dbo].[Portfolio_Valuation] AS [Extent4] ON ([Extent1].[Portfolio_Code] = [Extent4].[Portfolio_Code]) AND ([Extent1].[Entity_ID] = [Extent4].[Entity_ID])
        WHERE ([Extent1].[Entity_ID] = @p__linq__0) AND ((@p__linq__1 IS NULL) OR ([Extent1].[Portfolio_Name] LIKE @p__linq__2 ESCAPE '~'))
    )  AS [Project1]
    ORDER BY [Project1].[Portfolio_Name] ASC
